			<div class="user-review-heading">Good Cargo Bag - Works On 4 Point Roof Rack!</div>
			
				<div class="review-text">
					<p class="review-text-half">
						
						Had one of these for year ... 
						<a class="seemore" href="#">see more</a>
					</p>
					<p class="review-text-full hidden">
						Had one of these for years, a little advice:This works on roof racks that have side bars, and 2 sliding bars front/back. Put it forward on the rack so you can stand on the door sill to pack it.Best used with large rolling duffels since there is only 36&quot; x 36&quot; of area. Pack it full, having a corner flapping will make noise, and wear a hole. Fuse the ends of the straps with a match to prevent fraying.Check the tension on the straps every time you stop for gas.Tuck strap ends in to prevent noise and damage.Most repairs can be handled with black duct tape.

						This item seems to be fin ...

					</p>
					<p class="review-text-full hidden">
						This item seems to be fine, a little hard to connect the front tubing together during assembly. Works well with 3 bikes, will hold 4 with extra maneuvering due to the handle bars all hitting each other. Use a long thick cable through the bike frames and through the bike rack with a heavy duty lock and that would make it difficult for anyone to steel them. It works well in the truck bed as well as in the garage.
						<a class="seeless" href="#">see less</a>
					</p>

			<div class="user-ratings">
				<div class="rating-small twostar">
					<p class="ratings-current screen-reader-only">
						<strong>
								2 of 5 stars
						 </strong>
					</p>
				</div> 
				<span class="review-lbl-overall">overall</span>
			</div>
			
			
			
			<div class="user-review-heading">Cheap for a reason</div>
			
				<div class="review-text">
					<p class="review-text-half">
						
						We needed a cartop carrie ... 
						<a class="seemore" href="#">see more</a>
					</p>
					<p class="review-text-full hidden">
						We needed a cartop carrier at the last minute for a large SUV. We went with this one because it was in stock and didn't need crossbars (or at least that's what the instructions said). A few problems: the straps on the side of the carrier did not reach the side rails of our large SUV when we had it packed full. It might fit fine for a crossover or a small SUV. It has gone approximately 1600 miles (one round trip) through pretty good weather and is already starting to get holes in it. We also had to put a bungee cord across the back to keep it from sliding off the vehicle. It states it isn't waterproof. That's for sure. The 15 minutes of rain we went through got items in the carrier damp. I would hate to be using this in a downpour. The only plus is that it has a lot of room assuming you can get the side straps to reach. There might be good inexpensive carriers out there, but this isn't one of them.
						<a class="seeless" href="#">see less</a>
					</p>
				</div>
			
			<div class="review-info">
				<span class="author">W. Swift</span> Jul 17,11
			</div>
		</li>
	
	
	
		<li class="user-ratings-reviews">
			<div class="user-ratings">
				<div class="rating-small onestar">
					<p class="ratings-current screen-reader-only">
						<strong>
								1 of 5 stars
						 </strong>
					</p>
				</div>

			</div>
			
			
			
			<div class="user-review-heading">NOT MADE WELL</div>
			
				<div class="review-text">
					<p class="review-text-half">
						
						We bought this to use for ... 
						<a class="seemore" href="#">see more</a>
					</p>
					<p class="review-text-full hidden">
						We bought this to use for our vacation from Texas to Florida, and knew that it was only weather resistant, so we put our duffle bags in durable garbage bags, for extra protection, and then put it in the car carrier. By the time we got to Florida and took our luggage out of the karpak, the lining that makes it weather resistant had fallen apart, just crumbled, so now the only thing covering was the cloth of the actual carrier, so by the time we left Florida to go back to Texas you could see through the fabric and it was tearing holes. We used soft duffle bag luggage and not suit cases. Our clothes were totally dry because of the idea to put the bags in large garbage bags for protection, but I won't beable to use this luggage Highland KarPak again. I didn't have the cross bars, so even though it was buckled and strapped, it will slide to the back top of the car. I do not recommend the KarPak car top carrier by HIghland.
						<a class="seeless" href="#">see less</a>
					</p>
				</div>
			
			<div class="review-info">
				<span class="author">julie</span> Aug 22,12
			</div>
		</li>
